commit 3e1885ad38807f75e8cf45a7d7ccad0fe4412a86
Author: gmanipon <gmanipon@jpl.nasa.gov>
Date:   Fri May 30 14:41:53 2014 +0000

    Removed real-time GRQ update in datastager.
    Added reference checker code (Giangi's algorithm):
    
    "At this point you have the  metadata info into  FrameMetadata object. To create such  object do:
    
    from frameMetadata.FrameMetadata import FrameMetadata
    fm = FrameMetadata()
    fm.load(input) #the input could be the json
                   #file containing the metadata or the dictionary that you get
                   #by loading the json
    
    
    1. If fm.referece = False just save it to db
    2. If reference = True query for all the frames that have same fm.trackNumber
       and fm.beamID and have (latitudeIndexMax < fm.latitudeIndexMax + 3 and
       latitudeIndexMin > fm.latitudeIndexMin - 3) and reference = True
    3. If empty list than save it to db, and it will be the reference
    4. If the list contains something than loop through each result in the list,
       create a new FrameMetadata instance fm1 (from the dictionary you get as response)
       and call fm.IsInBbox(fm1.refbbox). If this returns false for all fm1 than save fm
       to db but flag fm since I will need to take a look because there is something suspicious.
    5. If one returns true than unpublished fm and rerun extractmetadata on fm. To be very
       pedantic loop through the all list an make sure that only one returned true. If more
       than one returns true don't save and flag fm so we can take a look."
    
    svn path=/trunk/ARIAMH-CCMODS/ariamh/; revision=7162
